  public\tmua-classes\index.html:111:

> public\tmua-classes\index.html:115:            <span>Next Live Session</span>

  public\tmua-classes\index.html:117:          </div>
  public\tmua-classes\index.html:118:          ${

  public\tmua-classes\index.html:122:          }
  public\tmua-classes\index.html:123:        </section>
  public\tmua-classes\index.html:124:

  public\tmua-classes\index.html:136:      `;

  public\tmua-classes\index.html:143:
  public\tmua-classes\index.html:144:        if (!res.ok || !data.ok) {

  public\tmua-classes\index.html:146:        }
  public\tmua-classes\index.html:147:
  public\tmua-classes\index.html:148:        render(data);
